Introduction

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://localhost:8000

Authenticating requests

Authenticate requests to this API's endpoints by sending an Authorization header with the value "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}".

All authenticated endpoints are marked with a requires authentication badge in the documentation below.

You can retrieve your token by visiting your dashboard and clicking Generate API token.

Activity Logs

Display a listing of the resource.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/activity_logs" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/activity_logs"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 47
vary: Origin

Request      

GET api/activity_logs

Authentication

Register

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/register" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"employee_id\": \"2019-001\",
    \"first_name\": \"Oliver\",
    \"last_name\": \"Pierce\",
    \"middle_name\": \"Mason\",
    \"suffix\": \"Jr.\",
    \"company_id\": 1,
    \"role_request\": \"admin\",
    \"email\": \"oliver.pierce@gmail.com\",
    \"password\": \"cmp5ZVpIMe\",
    \"confirmPassword\": \"cmp5ZVpIMe\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/register"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "employee_id": "2019-001",
    "first_name": "Oliver",
    "last_name": "Pierce",
    "middle_name": "Mason",
    "suffix": "Jr.",
    "company_id": 1,
    "role_request": "admin",
    "email": "oliver.pierce@gmail.com",
    "password": "cmp5ZVpIMe",
    "confirmPassword": "cmp5ZVpIMe"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/register

Body Parameters

employee_id  string  

Employee ID of the user.

first_name  string  

First name of the user.

last_name  string  

Last name of the user.

middle_name  string optional  

Middle name of the user.

suffix  string  

Suffix name of the user.

company_id  integer optional  

Company ID for the employees.

role_request  string optional  

Role request for the admins.

email  string  

email of the user.

password  string  

The value and confirmPassword must match.

confirmPassword  string  

confirm password.

Login

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"oliver.pierce@gmail.com\",
    \"password\": \"cmp5ZVpIMe\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "oliver.pierce@gmail.com",
    "password": "cmp5ZVpIMe"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/login

Body Parameters

email  string  

Email of the user.

password  required optional  

Password of the user.

Logout

requires authentication

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/logout" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {token}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/logout"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {token}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/logout

Category Management

APIs to manage the category resource.

Display a listing of the resource.

requires authentication

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/category" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {token}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/category"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {token}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Request      

GET api/category

Store a newly created resource in storage.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/category" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"Laptop\",
    \"spec\": [
        {
            \"name\": \"CPU\"
        }
    ]
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/category"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "Laptop",
    "spec": [
        {
            "name": "CPU"
        }
    ]
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",

Request      

GET api/company

Store a newly created resource in storage.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/company" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"Fligno AU\",
    \"acronym\": \"FAU\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/company"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "Fligno AU",
    "acronym": "FAU"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

GET api/remark

Store a newly created resource in storage.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/remark" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"unit\": \"ut\",
    \"name\": \"fuga\",
    \"date\": \"dolores\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/remark"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "unit": "ut",
    "name": "fuga",
    "date": "dolores"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

GET api/role/{id}

URL Parameters

id  integer  

The ID of the role.

Update the specified resource in storage.

Example request:
curl --request PUT \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/role/1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"permissions\": [
        11
    ]
}"

);

};

};

Request      

GET api/unit

Store a newly created resource in storage.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/unit" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"brand\": \"Intel\",
    \"model\": \"PTSE3U-06N006\",
    \"serial\": \"7H137673A\",
    \"details\": [
        {
            \"CPU\": \"Intel\",
            \"Memory\": \"8G\"
        }
    ],
    \"remarks\": [
        {
            \"name\": \"Defected Speaker\",
            \"date\": \"2022-09-09\"
        }
    ],
    \"company_id\": 1,
    \"category_id\": 1
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/unit"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "brand": "Intel",
    "model": "PTSE3U-06N006",
    "serial": "7H137673A",
    "details": [
        {
            "CPU": "Intel",
            "Memory": "8G"
        }
    ],
    "remarks": [
        {
            "name": "Defected Speaker",
            "date": "2022-09-09"
        }
    ],
    "company_id": 1,
    "category_id": 1
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
